Rev. Sun Myung Moon's Words Compilation Committee

Foreword
                   President of the World Peace Unification Family, Hwang Seon-jo

1)
Family
Matthew 10:34-39
<Prayer> Merciful Father, may Your glory be with us on this second Sabbath of the month.
At this time, we wish to offer our inadequate selves before You, and we hope that You will accept us as a whole. We dedicate all the twists and circumstances that humanity has endured throughout history entirely to You, and we ask that You allow us to be individuals who can uphold the environment You desire.
May this time be one where we can reaffirm our relationship with You, our True Father, and with each other. Also, may it be a time where each of us can pledge to fulfill the responsibilities and missions You have entrusted to us.
There are countless people living on this earth, and while some claim to know You, we know that many more do not. Among those who know You, there are very few who truly understand Your intentions and strive to fulfill and spread them, and we are well aware of the fact that those who take on the responsibility of being true individuals are exceedingly rare.
Among the many nations, may You remember this pitiful Korean people, and among this nation, may You remember the unfortunate children. We, gathered here, have traversed many twists and turns. We have walked the sorrowful path, paving the way through struggles. We have not come this way for anyone else, but we have come to this place following the path You have guided us on.
Now is the time to clearly understand what Your desire is in sending us, and we ask that You allow us to realize the significant responsibility we have to align our desires with Yours, so that we may return to You with the results of that desire.
Father, as Your children gather here, if there are any sorrows You have faced throughout the ages, we ask that You appeal to each of our hearts. If there are injustices and grievances in our confrontation with the enemy, we earnestly wish for You to instill in us the determination to seek retribution and forgiveness for all of it. Since we began through You, we wish to live through You. Therefore, may this time be one where Your power and the strength of life surge within each of our hearts as we offer everything before You and follow.
We must step over the difficulties of this nation. We also understand the heavy responsibility we have as those who have received the heavenly command to resolve all chaotic circumstances, so we must be thorough in our sense of purpose. When the enemy obstructs this purpose, we must push through that enemy, and when the environment responds, we must remove that environment. We earnestly wish to become Your sons and daughters who can recognize the need for individuals who are determined in this resolution.
When You called us out of the countless people, we know that there was a great purpose in it. We understand that there was a special intention to bestow upon us Your mission and to command a new mission. Father, therefore, we earnestly wish for You to allow each of us to fully dedicate our bodies and minds before You, so that we may embody the appearance of heavenly warriors racing toward the final front lines.
To become heavenly warriors, we must equip ourselves with both internal and external preparations, and we must also understand all the skills the enemy possesses. Without this understanding, we know we cannot achieve victory in that battle. As we set forth this year with the slogan of full-scale advance once again, we must become Your sons and daughters who embody the appearance of heavenly warriors and add advance upon advance. We wish to become Your children who strive with all their efforts toward the place of Your desire, the place where You aim, overcoming the difficult circumstances and lonely positions we find ourselves in, and we earnestly hope for this, Father.
Today is a holy Sabbath. Please bless the countless children who call upon Your holy name scattered throughout the world. Among them, please remember the children of unification who kneel alone and worship before You, following the ties of Your heart.
We believe that many children in Korea are worshiping before You at this time, so please be with them there, and grant them strength and power as they fight to restore and return the mission You have entrusted to them while longing for the headquarters, Father, we earnestly wish for this.
We have come before You at this time, so please personally oversee everything. Allow nothing other than You to dominate our hearts and bodies. Only You must preside. The ties of our nature long to exist eternally with You, and the heart of our nature wishes to serve for Your purpose eternally, so please allow this time to deepen our relationship with You, and let the hearts of those who convey and receive the words become one.
At this time, we earnestly request that everything begins through You and that the results come from You. We earnestly ask that You personally preside until the remaining time is over, and we offer all these words in the name of the True Parents. Amen.
<Words> There are countless people living in this world, and they all belong to families. However, without true families, it is impossible to raise true children, and the formation of a true society is also impossible. Thus, it is a natural fact that true societies, nations, and worlds are formed through true families.
What should we pursue?
Until now, education, cultivation, and religion have focused on the individual. Although we have gone through a long historical process, we can conclude that no one has achieved the complete individual and formed a complete family that surpasses all the standards of morality and culture that have been emphasized throughout history.
Any great figures or saints who desire a world beyond their aspirations must first practice that ideal themselves; it cannot be realized naturally in any space. It is an undeniable fact that they must first enact it, develop it, and expand it. Thus, it is unnecessary to say that they must first act upon themselves, then transfer it to their families, to their tribes, and ultimately to the world.
Throughout the historical age, there has been no clear definition of what a true family is. Moreover, the goals and limitations that a true person should aim for have not been clearly defined. Humanity finds itself in a process where it does not know where it came from or where it is going. And this humanity has passed through history without defining the standards for the purpose it must reach, the criteria for cultivation, and the limits of human perfection. Therefore, it is also undeniable that it has not formed the standard of a perfect personality that can connect all of history and the future. Because individuals have not reached such a position, it is impossible for humanity to form the highest familial standards it desires.
In this light, while it is a problem that countless humans are struggling on their respective life paths, we must not forget the greater issue that the problem of establishing familial standards based on individuals remains on the path of humanity's progress and development. This is the starting point for families that can run toward the original homeland that humanity aims for, on the fundamental trajectory. Without this, we must understand that it is impossible to reach the ideal world that all humanity yearns for and the purpose they seek.
Then, what is the ultimate goal that religion should aim for? While it is valid to assert the purpose of individual asceticism, it must go further to seek families. First, we must find families to liberate humanity, which is under the dominion of evil, from sin. We must find families that truly represent history, the times, and the future. Furthermore, we must establish the foundation of a family that all of humanity can rejoice in and the standard of the path (the right way) that families must follow. It must be determined where the system of that family originates and where it should go. Without this, it is impossible to establish a world of peace on this earth. We must understand that even if external matters are well accomplished, they can collapse when it comes to the internal family.
The source of happiness and the point where God's love can manifest as reality
When we call someone a happy person in human life, what criteria do we use to define happiness? Can we say that someone is happy just because they possess some external ability, power, or authority? No, we cannot. Is a person with enough money to not envy anyone considered happy? No, they are not. Can someone with global knowledge and in a position to influence the world be considered a happy person? Certainly not; that alone does not make a person happy.
While all humans on this earth generally feel, experience, and recognize that the foundation of happiness is family, they still lack the standards for a happy family. This is something we must recognize as a problem. Therefore, the issue lies with the family. A family must have parents. In the world, children without parents are called orphans, and those orphans are treated as pitiful individuals. A family must have parents, and at the same time, there must be a bond between spouses. While it is unfortunate to be without parents, it is also unfortunate if one spouse is missing. No matter how lovingly a couple lives together, losing a beloved partner leads to immense misery and unhappiness. Furthermore, if a couple cannot have children, that too is an undeniable misfortune.
Even if someone does not succeed in society or lacks the authority and qualifications as a member of society, if they can create a family centered around true parents, true spouses, and true children, living peacefully to the extent that anyone would want to emulate that family, then that family is undeniably a happy family.
Such a family should not be limited to true happiness within the family; it must also influence society, relatives, clans, tribes, and ultimately the nation and state. If such a family exists, it will undoubtedly be a family that the entire nation or state admires. If a family can represent a nation and further transcend to be admired by the world, then all of humanity will surely revere that family.
Throughout history, many have revered saints and sages, yet what has been the point of peace in the ideal family they desire, the family they wish to love, and the family centered around filial piety and loving spouses? When asked this, there is no answer.
Then, what is the ultimate foundation of happiness that humanity seeks? It is the heart. When we observe that happiness and unhappiness are determined based on emotional foundations, the question arises: what is the emotional foundation of a true family that can prove God, religion, and the issue of the soul, and influence the environment?
You all know the saying, "God is love." Where should that love manifest? Where should it manifest? Everyone wishes for it to manifest in themselves. However, if that love only appears to one person, it ends with that individual. If it manifests only to a man or a woman, it will all be gone within a century. In other words, if one person cannot deepen that love and pass it on before they die, it can only be a love that ends with one generation.
So, how can we establish the standard of eternal bloodline love? If the love of God, which appears to one man and one woman, can be instilled in the children who are formed through that family bond, then from there, eternal love can manifest in humanity. In other words, the point where the intangible love of God can manifest as reality will appear. In this light, we cannot deny that the overall foundation for realizing God's love ultimately culminates in the family.
The point of humanity's salvation
In modern society, youth issues are causing controversy not only in South Korea but globally. So, what is the motivation behind their situation? More than 80%, 90%, or even 100% of that motivation lies in emotional issues. It stems from not having good parents, not having good siblings, and deficiencies in male-female relationships, which have led to such outcomes.
Considering this fact, what is the standard that can rectify all these ailments? It is also found in the family.
Throughout the history of this world, there have been countless revolutions. Even if many facts have moved the world as a result of those revolutions, they all eventually pass. The final issue is that a center capable of initiating a revolution to establish true families must manifest on this earth. From there, a new world must emerge, and a new historical ideal must begin; this is an undeniable fact.
In light of these issues, each of you must consider a question. If a person does not have the origin of a proper family, where will they go? Even if they go somewhere, they will inevitably return without finding a stable destination.
the world would be plunged into darkness and chaos. Life as we know it would cease to exist. Yet, we take the sun for granted, just as we do with love and family.

In this context, the ideal family that humanity longs for must emerge. This family must be the model, the standard that we aspire to, yet we have not even achieved a basic level of what a family should be. We are not even at a score of 10 out of 100; rather, we are in a negative state, akin to a minus 100 score. Hearing this might be upsetting, and while it may be uncomfortable for you to hear, it is even more uncomfortable for me to say. Living in a minus 100 family while claiming to be happy is a contradiction. The more we try to find happiness in such a family, the more we realize we are in a deep pit of unhappiness.

We must establish a family that serves as a model. Should we just sit idly by and watch such families exist? Or should we break them apart? I am not suggesting that you go home tonight and destroy your family. (Laughter) While it is necessary to break apart the flawed structures, we must have a plan for reconstruction. Even if we break something, we must have a solution in place before doing so. Do you understand?

If God intends to use a family as a model to guide other families, then He will establish that model family and break apart the flawed ones. This act of breaking is not evil. Do you understand? It is natural for negative phenomena to occur at the crossroads of transforming a world of evil into a world of true happiness. If God is a God of love, He can break apart the flawed structures while providing a solution. I support this. What about you? From the looks in your eyes, it seems you all agree.

Some may think, "I don't understand this yet, so how can I agree?" However, once you hear these words, you cannot help but agree. 

When that model family emerges, will you follow it or not? Those who do not follow will fail. And they deserve to fail. If you understand my words, you will not be upset by this. Therefore, you must follow, no matter what happens.

Looking at the eyes of Koreans, they stand out compared to people from other countries. We are the most prominent people in the world in terms of eye prominence. Among Asians, Koreans have particularly prominent eyes. Why is that? There may be exceptions like me, but when we look at Westerners, their eyes are generally recessed. In the past, those with recessed eyes were more successful because they had to think deeply. However, in this time, we need to have prominent eyes. In the end times, we cannot afford to keep our eyes closed. (Laughter)

From this perspective, Koreans can see further than people from any other country. (Laughter) Considering this, even if we fight with our eyes, noses, and mouths, we will not lose. (Laughter) Westerners may struggle to see with one eye, but Asians can see with one eye and still see the other. (Laughter) We are indeed beautiful people. (Laughter)

Traveling around Southeast Asia, when you see someone with prominent eyes, you can tell they are Korean. This shows the incredible ability of God's harmony. When we think that Koreans have been placed in a position to see well in the end times, it brings a mix of feelings, both unpleasant and uplifting.

So, if there is a flawed family as I mentioned earlier, should we just leave it alone, or should we break it apart? Those who find my words provocative may suggest we should wait and see. But that is not the right approach. We must break it apart.

Let’s break it! The phrase "let's break it" feels more real than just saying "let's break it." 

What did Jesus come to do? What did the saints and sages come to do? It is a question that cannot be overlooked. If there were a well-functioning family, we would be encouraged to emulate it, but until now, such families have not existed.

Have there been any serious thinkers who contemplated the ideal that humanity has longed for? Did Buddha think deeply about this? Did Confucius? Who has seriously considered this? We must think deeply about the fact that if there is a power to save humanity centered around a true family, that power must originate from the family itself. If such a thinker exists, he would undoubtedly be a great religious leader and a savior who can guide all of humanity to one place. But has this happened in Buddhist or Confucian thought? Confucianism does not address the essence of God. While Confucianism promotes the idea of Heaven, the "Heaven" it refers to is not a personal being with love, hence it cannot have a close relationship with humanity.

What about Jesus? Where did His teachings come from? He did not say, "Live by doing good deeds and you will go to heaven." Instead, He said, "I am the way, the truth, and the life. No one comes to the Father except through me." (John 14:6) Jesus did not say to be a learner, but rather to follow Him. By following Him, Christians become like Jesus.

Did you learn how to love in your family? Did any father tell his children to learn how to love him? Did you receive such education? Did mothers tell their children to learn how to love them? Who taught parents how to love their children? Who taught brides and grooms how to love? You may not have learned it formally, but you do it well. It is a mysterious thing. All humans do not learn it, yet they do it well.

You know that air exists, right? You breathe it every day, but do you say, "Ah, this is air!" while living? You live without even thinking about the air you breathe. Everyone receives sunlight daily, but have you ever expressed gratitude to the sunlight in the morning and evening? Did you learn how to greet the sun? It seems you have not learned that either. (Laughter)

Water is the same. Did anyone teach you how to drink water? Did you learn how to drink? It seems you have not learned that either. We do not learn about the most precious things.

Now, let’s think about the sun, which is the most precious. What would happen if the sun disappeared for just two days? Can you even imagine it?
The air is the same. Right now, humans are shouting loudly, but if we were to disappear from the Earth for just about 15 minutes, and the air decided to go on a strike in alliance, what would happen? On such a day, world unity could be achieved easily. There would be no need to put up a sign saying "Unification Church." It's simple. World unity would be accomplished in less than 10 minutes, not even 15.

Have you learned how to breathe air or drink water? You naturally know how to do it without learning. Everything precious in the world is like that. If God exists, He must be far more precious than those things. How can humans know Him? Similarly, they come to know God without learning. Originally, it is said that one should know about God without being taught.

Do you know how big your heart is? It is not visible, but it exists. This heart is so big that it probably wouldn't be satisfied even if you put a hundred or a thousand worlds inside it. Also, if you were given just one diamond like the Earth, you would feel bad. The heart is unimaginably vast.

Moreover, your heart knows good and bad without learning. Did your heart learn that if someone does this or that, it is bad, then you should be a watchman? You haven't learned it, but the heart does not care if the body is big and strong. Rather, it reacts immediately, even faster than electricity, in proportion to that strength. If you think differently, it stops immediately. How much education would it take for that to happen? If a person could be educated to be like that at any time, it would be a great success. No matter how great an educator is, they have not been able to do this. So, have you experienced this learning or not? Everyone knows and does it well without learning.

The best and most precious thing in this world is God's love. God loved the world so much that He gave His only begotten Son, so that whoever believes in Him shall not perish but have eternal life. Why is that necessary? It is necessary because humans are not in God's love; if they were, what would be the use? If someone clearly got married, how would it feel if you kept saying they got married? After just three times, it would feel bad.

God is a God of love, but does He teach humans not to take the most precious thing from Him? No. If that were the case, He would be a God who teaches theft. It is not that God taught and humans came to know. They come to know without being taught. God's love is like this, but why have humans not been able to become like that? What is the motivation behind that thought, and from whom does it come?

When looking at such issues, eating from the tree of the knowledge of good and evil is not an absolute sin. Setting other issues aside, the fall from eating the fruit of that tree is absolutely not the case. It is not a matter of love; one cannot transcend death without it. This is evident even from common sense. Until now, pastors have said that humans fell after eating from the tree of the knowledge of good and evil, resulting in original sin. So, what exactly is original sin? What is it?

Becoming God's firstborn son
When thinking about this, it is said that the fall happened because of the issue of love. The law of love, which should have started centered on God, and the ethics of love went wrong, so it needs to be corrected. The starting point of humanity did not begin centered on the absolute God but started illegally. Thus, families, nations, and the world were formed. Because the family that God desired could not be established, we must seek such families. Therefore, you should understand that your family members are enemies.

So, among the religious leaders, who has seriously thought about such families? That person is Jesus. Jesus said, "Follow me." If you follow Him, you will understand. The position of the leader of Christianity is a difficult one. Moreover, the saints are not just learners; they are followers. Therefore, those who struggle to follow Jesus, who died on the cross, and decide to walk the path of death will be the first to arrive in heaven. Thus, the secret to going to heaven is simple.

So, what did Jesus say about God? He said that God is not the father of friends, nor the ruler of nations, nor any global ruler. He said, "God is my Father." Not only that, but He also said He is the only begotten Son of God. If God exists, there must be a Son, and Jesus is the firstborn and only Son. It feels uncomfortable. It would make the father feel uncomfortable too. How would a father feel if his son said, "Father! I am your only begotten Son, so do not call me a bastard"? How upset would that father be? (Laughter) From the beginning, Jesus said, "God is my Father, and I am His only begotten Son."

So, who is the closest person to God? Who is it? "It's me." Is that enough? (Laughter) Then, you become Jesus. Just saying that would feel good. You answered very well.

Did the loving God truly love humans? Some of you may not know whether God exists, so what kind of love is that? If God loves me, from what position would He love me? Think about it. If God loves a human who is like a beggar or a thug, then that is a wrong God. If He is a God of love, what kind of person would He want to love? What position would that person be in?

When someone gets married and wants to have children, would you prefer to have a daughter first or a son? Please answer, everyone here. Is it better to have a first son or a first daughter? "A first son is better." Where did you learn that? Even if you didn't learn it from anyone, you know it well. There is no need to ask men with a thief's mindset. (Laughter) When a first son is born, they are happy without saying a word and drooling with joy. It is said that it is permissible to hit someone who has given birth to a first son and make them treat you to a meal. Looking at this, our Korean customs are good.

In this way, whether it is a boy or a girl, if you are going to have a child, you want to have a first son. Would you prefer a son who says to his father, "I will be the youngest son"? Or would you prefer a son who grabs his father's collar and says, "I will be the firstborn"? What do you think?

God would also prefer someone who insists on being the firstborn, even if it means grabbing His collar. In this regard, we can understand that God approves of Jacob taking the birthright from Esau.

When God loves people, from what position does He love them? What kind of human does the God of love love the most? It is precisely those who are in a father-son relationship.

Jesus was also very ambitious. He said that even as a son, He would be the firstborn. Because the firstborn was taken away, the world became a problem. What will you become? Will you be the firstborn? What do you want to be? If Jesus became the firstborn, you cannot. Does that make you uncomfortable? Then you must fight to take the firstborn position from Jesus. Even if Jesus became the firstborn, if you bring out conditions that allow you to be the older brother, Jesus must yield.

Until now, Jesus has been God's firstborn. So, what will you become? Will you be a servant? Today, Christians pray, "Please bless your servant." If you are going to pray, why not pray as a servant of a servant? I feel uncomfortable, so I do not pray like that. Unification Church members must never pray like that. If a son goes home to eat and says to his father, "Father, here comes the servant," would that father feel good? (Laughter) That would be infuriating. "Oh, let this house be whatever it will be!" Such a sigh would escape. Therefore, we Unification Church members must never pray while calling ourselves servants. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." But do not teach this to established Christians. (Laughter) Then we can exchange opinions with those who oppose us once more.

If God is the essence of love, then there must be a father-son relationship with humans. If there is another relationship, then He is not a God of love. That is why in Christianity, God could be called Father.

Jesus, who came to receive a bride
Jesus said, "I am the bridegroom, and you are the bride." So, what does the bride and bridegroom want to do? What do they want to do? They want to get married. They want to establish a family. If they cannot have children, that family cannot even be considered a family. (Laughter) If they cannot have children, they will start to fall apart. Only after having children can a family be firmly established. Even if the bride hates him and wants to divorce him, if they have only given birth to sons, that bridegroom has no choice but to stay together. Therefore, to establish a family, there must be children.

So, if Jesus comes as the bridegroom and we are to be the bride, what should we, as the brides, do? Is the purpose of the bride and bridegroom to live looking at the front and back hills, saying, "Dear bridegroom, dear bride"? Without thinking of the true content, the bride says, "Even though I am so unattractive, please accept me as your first-class bride." That is being greedy without knowing one's place.

Jesus came to this earth as God's only begotten Son and as the prince of the heavenly kingdom. He came as the first prince of God. He is the son who was born worthy of inheriting God's full authority. The Jewish people should have welcomed such a son of God and become God's first daughter-in-law, but they could not do that. However, when we look at today's Christians, they outwardly pray, "Dear bridegroom!" but when they see Jesus, they think, "How can the bridegroom be so shabby?"

Are there people here who pray like servants? They just say, "Dear bridegroom, I am about to die, so please save me." Looking at this, it is astonishing. When things are good for them, they act as if they do not know, but when they are in trouble and sad, they cry out, "Lord!" This is how families fall apart.

Jesus is the first prince of God. Then, among you, is there anyone who is confident they can become the bride of that prince? Raise your hand if you are confident. Even if you raise your hand, you are worried, right? (Laughter) If you ask established Christians what it means to become a bride and bridegroom, they will say, "What do you mean? It means to go to heaven." Then, if you ask, "What happens in heaven?" they cannot answer. You cannot believe like that.

When we delve into all these issues, the conclusion is that the bride and bridegroom must establish a family. Is there any objection to this? Is there anyone who dislikes that? The bride and bridegroom must regard God as their Father and form a relationship as the prince and princess of heaven. Establishing a family centered on God was Jesus' wish. Otherwise, what would Jesus' wish have been? Would it have been to own the world?

No matter how much Jesus could control the world, He could not achieve this family standard. When we look at this, what is Jesus' wish? Because He came as the bridegroom, He must receive a bride. Because He came as the heavenly prince, He must receive a daughter-in-law of God who can replace the heavenly princess. Isn't this a clear principle? Even those who are new can accept this as a clear principle once they understand it. However, until now, Christianity has not believed this way.

So, what should Christianity do? The heavenly prince came to establish His position, but they drove Him away, so they must apologize a thousand or ten thousand times. And all of humanity must prepare a bride for the one they collectively desire to come and create the environment He wishes. This historical responsibility is what the religion of Christianity, as the bride, must bear. This is what Christians must do. If they desire something else, they are all thieves.

What Jesus had to accomplish when He came
In this way, what Christians must prepare is the first purpose that Jesus desired. Before achieving this first purpose, we humans cannot accomplish the second purpose. Can you go to heaven if you believe in Jesus and succeed in business? You cannot go to heaven like that. That is why Jesus said it is harder for a camel to go through the eye of a needle.

What is Jesus' first purpose? It is to receive a bride. It is to hold a feast for the Lamb. What is this feast for the Lamb? As it is written in the Bible, it is a feast where God's first prince receives a bride and begins a household.

Then, what will be done with that feast? Christians believe they will float up into the air on clouds. Even if these Christians are smart, they cannot be any smarter than that. (Laughter)

After the first prince of God brings the bride and holds the feast for the Lamb, should He go up into the sky on clouds or live on the earth? If they have found the one they were looking for, they should dance right there or at least take a look. Why do all the well-believing Christians take everyone up and have a feast in the air? What kind of feast in the air is that? Where are they going up to? Nowadays, one might go up with a satellite, but ultimately, they have to come back down. They are going up to float in the air, not to go anywhere.

Ultimately, Jesus' purpose is to obtain a bride and establish a family. Those who do not understand this might say, "I went to the Unification Church, and that Mr. Moon said that Jesus needs to establish a family." They might feel uncomfortable hearing that. Then, they probably thought they would become the first-class bride or special bride and float up into the sky on clouds, right? However, since the principles are set, there is no other way.

The issue is family. If a family is established, what must Jesus become? He must become the head of the family. At the same time, He must become the family leader. He must become the family master. So, to what standard has Jesus come? He has not even established a family. The family Jesus intended to establish is different from the families you are living in today. The families you are living in are not the right families. They are families that have gone wrong for 6,000 years.

However, the family that Jesus was to establish is one that God would be pleased with, a family that could live for thousands and tens of thousands of years. In one of our folk songs, there is a line that goes, "Oh bright moon, the moon that Lee Taebaek played with, in that moon over there, the sweetgum tree is stuck, so bring my parents and let them live for thousands and tens of thousands of years." Koreans sing this well.
It has been said that this is not a song of a Korean person but rather a song that God wants to sing. If such a family is formed, is it a family that has been established or not? The problem is that it has not become such a family.

True Religion in the Restoration Providence
<Summary of the Message> What is true religion? 
First, it is a religion that monopolizes God's love. Therefore, the being that governs that religion must also be able to monopolize God's love. What kind of being can monopolize God's love? Humans love their own creations. Therefore, if there is someone who loves and likes their own works, that person will also be loved and liked in return. In the same way, if there is someone who loves and appreciates God's creations more than God does, God will love that person the most and will want to fully inherit all His possessions, power, and love to that person.

However, the only being that can love and cherish everything of God more than God Himself is God's son. Therefore, the being that God loves the most is the son who serves God as his Father, and that son is the being who can monopolize God's love.

The son who monopolizes God's love has equal dominion with God. Thus, we can see that Adam in the Garden of Eden, who was to be the true father of humanity, is the embodiment of God with equal rights to God. This religion of the son, the religion that monopolizes God's love, is the truest religion.

May 19, 1969 (Mon), Chuncheon Church. 
* This message was given at the last visited area of the national tour after returning from the world tour and was compiled from what was published in <Gangwon News>. The title was added by the editor.

Second, a religion that seeks the masterpiece that has monopolized God's love is true religion. In other words, a religion that seeks to find God's son and establish a connection with him is true religion. A religion that denies the body centered on the heart to establish a new connection, denies the past connections centered on the new connection, and denies this world centered on new families, new nations, and new worlds is true religion.

Third, a religion that reveals God's love is true religion. A religion that reveals God's love through parental love, through spousal love, and through children's love is true religion.

Then, what kind of religion is it that denies the world to find God's son and reveals God's love? It is Christianity. Jesus proclaimed God as Father and declared Himself as the Son of God, which speaks of a deep moral level. Furthermore, Jesus said, "Whoever wants to follow me must deny themselves and take up their cross," and "Love me more than anyone else."

Also, when we see that He will return at the end as the King of Kings, with the glory of the Father and love, we can understand that Christianity is the truest religion. Therefore, we pray in the name of the True Parents.

Why is Jesus without original sin? 
Sin is allowing conditions for Satan to accuse. Satan can accuse humans because humans have a blood relationship with Satan. Therefore, the restoration providence aims to change the blood relationship caused by good and evil.

The first trace of the providence of restoration is found in the family of Adam. God wanted to separate Adam, who was in a position of mixed good and evil, into Cain, who was in a position of evil bloodline, and Abel, who was in a position of good bloodline, to carry out the blood restoration providence. If Abel had won there, he would have restored the good bloodline, and the Messiah could have come on that foundation. However, since Cain won, the bloodline of sin continued to propagate.

The second trace of restoration providence is found in the family of Abraham. God gave twins to Isaac, giving rise to Esau, in the position of Cain, and Jacob, in the position of Abel, to restore the birthright. Jacob, after finishing 21 years of wilderness life in Haran, subdued the angel, symbolizing spiritual Satan, at the Jabbok River and returned home to subdue Esau, symbolizing physical Satan. Because he stood in the position of having restored the birthright for the first time in history, God gave him the name Israel, meaning "victor."

To the victorious son of Jacob, Judah, God again gave twins to restore the birthright from the womb, which is the restoration providence through Perez and Zerah. By pushing aside Zerah, who was in the position of the firstborn, and having Perez, who was in the position of the secondborn, be born first, the good bloodline of Perez subdued Zerah, who was in the position of evil, restoring the position of the firstborn. In this way, Jesus was born through the victorious good bloodline.

The reason God did not allow Jesus to be born right away was due to the indemnity period, and because at that time, the world of Satan was forming a national structure, He wanted to restore it on a national basis, which is why He allowed 2,000 years to pass before Jesus was born. Therefore, Jesus was of the good bloodline from birth, and Satan could not accuse Him.

What is the nature of the second seven-year course? 
God completed the creation of all things in five days and created humans on the sixth day, resting on the seventh day. If all things and humans had been completed as created, the first day of all things, the day of children, the day when Adam and Eve, the parents of humanity, would have completed and entered the position of parents, and finally, the day when God could rest would have been established. However, due to the fall, none of those days could be established, so the restoration providence is to find those days.

Our Unification Church established the first seven-year course from 1960 to 1967 to restore the lost days. In 1960, we established the days of parents and children, and in 1963, we established the day of all things. After this seven-year course ended, on January 1, 1968, we finally welcomed the year of God's rest and proclaimed God's day. Up until this point was the first seven-year course, the course of parents.

And from 1968, the second seven-year course began, marking the start of the course of children. Children must walk based on the path their parents walked as an example. They must restore the lost children of faith to receive the blessings of their parents and receive the blessings of all things to inherit the mission and welcome the year of rest. If this is not accomplished in these seven years, it must be extended to 21 years.

What must be understood in the second seven-year course is that God's day is the day when the True Parents appear as the embodiment of God, and it is the day when Satan, who did not submit to humans, submits to the parents who have clothed themselves in the embodiment of God. By establishing this day of God, the condition was set for angels to submit to Adam and for Cain to submit to Abel.

The second seven-year course is a period that starts from the position of the restored firstborn. In the past, we faced persecution because we had to take the position of the firstborn from the position of the secondborn, but now we are in the position of sharing blessings from the position of the firstborn, so we will not be hated or persecuted. That time has come. Now, if there is disobedience, we must remember that the responsibility lies with the firstborn to restore them as children of heaven, even if it means using force. Just as the parents worked historically with the mission of the Messiah in the first seven-year course, in the second seven-year course, you must fulfill the mission of the Messiah for the restoration of your tribes.

Father, before we say that your love is like this, please allow us to know that your circumstances are like this. Let us be your children who understand that there were many circumstances in the past that were even more miserable than your current situation. When we look at ourselves, let us recognize that we are shameful before you, and allow us to be the ones who should comfort you.

External hometown and internal hometown
Even if the hometown changes, we know that the heart that yearns for the hometown does not change. Moreover, we also know that the highest places, like tall mountain peaks or towering rocks, are things we can never forget and wish to boast about.

Then, if God created this world and established a homeland of love where humanity can enjoy happiness, what would the countless spirits who have come and gone with this homeland boast about when they reach the other world? It would be the same as when you leave your hometown and long for it. Just as you want to stay up all night listening to the stories of relatives or friends in your hometown, if today this world had become an ideal homeland of heaven that God could love and be pleased with, then for the spirits passing through this land, this place must be the homeland.

No matter how good the spirit world may be, we must understand that the connections with the environment in which we grew up and all the relatives we spent time with in that land, whether as a nation or as humanity, are incredibly close to the spirits.

Once gone, while it is possible to return spiritually, from the standpoint of having a physical presence, one can never appear on this earth again. Therefore, all the environments and emotional connections woven through the experiences felt on this earth will become conditions for praise along with their eternal life and will be conditions for boasting before all their companions in the eternal heaven.

Considering this fact, if this earth had not been separated and had realized heaven, then the countless spirits who have passed through this earth would be able to boast about this place just as we individuals want to boast about our hometown. Spirits also want to relate themselves to high places if there are any, and they want to relate themselves to scenic spots if there are any.

From this perspective, if there are world-famous scenic spots, those places will inevitably become places that countless spirits in the spirit world long for and can boast about.

Just as the external natural environment on earth is so, when viewed from the perspective of emotional issues, the various stories intertwined with parents, siblings, and relatives in the hometown become objects of longing and conditions for boasting for the many spirits who come and go on this earth.

During our time on this earth, if we have a heartwarming emotional story that we can boast about before God, that story must also be one that we can eternally boast about.

For this reason, people wish to be well-regarded in appearance and want to be the possessors of deep emotional hearts more than anyone else. Today, as we long for our hometown, we hope to be able to boast of the emotional connections intertwined with our family, parents, or siblings, and just as we want to boast about special places in our hometown, it is undeniable that we also want to boast about our external and internal appearances. Therefore, it is a natural desire for humans to want to be patriots who love their country more than anyone else and to enjoy popularity in that country.

The heart of parents must become an unchanging form
We will all go to the spirit world in the future. Living on this earth is temporary, but the spirit world is the eternal world, the unchanging world. Therefore, when we go to that unchanging world, we must predict that we cannot boast with a changing appearance.

When we consider why our Unification Church has come to think of the inner circumstances of all humanity centered on the heart of parents, we see that things like brotherly love or national love can change with the external environment. Only the heart of parents does not change. Therefore, the unchanging heart of parents remains as a relative heart that can match the rhythm in the other world, that is, the eternal world. Moreover, if there is a natural environment that was loved through that heart, that natural environment will also remain as a counterpart of the unchanging heart.

What we will never forget in our lives is not the scenic spots themselves but a place filled with stories that are emotionally intertwined and unforgettable. We know that we will long for that place throughout our lives and recall it throughout our lives. Why is that? It is because there is an unchanging true love connected to it.

This nation and this people must not regress. They must develop forever and prosper forever. However, when the nation faces misfortune and is in crisis, if there are traces of patriotism that wish to save the nation with all their loyalty and devotion, those traces are not only personal traces but become traces that can be recognized before the nation when they are equipped with the content that can be remembered in the hearts of the entire people. In other words, they will remain eternally in the hearts of the nation and will be remembered forever by that nation. We can understand that this becomes a foundation of such heart by looking at historical facts.

From this perspective, while living on the earth, you must understand that you need to have such connections with those objects.

If I have loved my children with the heart of a parent in the true sense, I can boast about it. If I have given birth to and raised my children with the heart of a parent in the true sense, and if I loved them to create the pillars of the nation, how much did I love them? More than the nation, more than my spouse, more than any relatives, and more than my siblings, if I loved them, then that is something I can boast about.

Such love is not something taught by anyone. That love is a love that cannot be avoided. From this perspective, the love I have for my children is something that no one can take away and that no one can deny. The more time and devotion have been invested in it, the more so. The heart that cherishes children, hopes for them, and wants to be with them forever is the same for everyone. Even if parents are in such a position, if there is even a slight sign of unfilial behavior or change from the children, we must understand that all the love the parents have had for their children until now can become a trigger for an explosion of emotions and a motive for sorrow.

In this light, just because a parent has loved their child does not mean that they can live in God's homeland. After loving their children, they must love their siblings as they love their children, love their families as they love their children, love their nations as they love their children, and love the world as they love their children.

The unchanging standard of parental love

And we must understand that this standard can remain as an eternal standard in the future.

For this reason, when we ask what the standard will be for the ideal world, that is, the kingdom of heaven on earth, we must understand that it is the heart of parents. You must know that the kingdom of heaven on earth cannot be realized apart from the heart of parents.

The central thought of the Unification Church

If you add seven years for each of the three stages of rebirth, growth, and completion, it totals 21 years, which is 20 years in terms of the lunar calendar. In Korean age, it is 21 years old, and in lunar terms, it is 20 years old; this is when humans enter maturity. When one reaches maturity, the loving God will automatically arrange marriages.

Adam and Eve were to receive blessings centered on God and become the true parents of humanity, but they failed to do so. Love and dominion. When you grow through rebirth, growth, and completion, you will enter the realm of indirect dominion. Direct dominion is established centered on God. God said to love because humanity must learn to love in order to meet God, who loves humanity, and to align with the way of love. This is a preparation for that.

The history up to now has been the history of the restoration of the firstborn. Originally, the second born is to be under the dominion of the firstborn. The second born is one step lower than the firstborn in terms of stages. However, this principle is being overturned. The second born is to gain the position of the firstborn, and the firstborn is to be made to take the position of the second born. **The Attitude of a Minister**

<Summary of the Message> A minister (evangelist) must have experience above all else and should be able to create a shocking emotional response in the person being evangelized. When preaching, there are those who receive grace and those who do not; the issue is how to narrow that gap. To bridge that gap, the person who has received grace should be mobilized to prepare the ground for those who have not. In other words, the person who has received grace should put in sincerity for those who have not.

When dealing with members (the evangelized), approach them with interest and affection, and engage them in a fun manner. First, one must be immersed in their own purpose so that it can be conveyed to the other person. When dealing with members, even if it gets late, do not miss the precious opportunity to elevate grace, and give your best regardless of time. If you stop speaking when grace is at its peak because you are worried about time, you will have to start over from the beginning the next day.

May 1969, Seorak-myeon, Gapyeong-gun, Gyeonggi-do.

* This message was delivered during the first special training session for regional leaders that started on May 27, 1969, and has been compiled from what was published in the 23rd issue of <Kisoo> (June 1969). The title was added by the editor.

Core members should put in sincerity even if it means staying up all night. If they put in sincerity for just three days, that person will form an unforgettable bond of grace for a lifetime. Even if the person being evangelized has to leave because it is late, if the evangelist expresses regret and sorrow, the spiritual world will cooperate.

If you have done your utmost sincerity but the leader does not recognize you while recognizing someone inferior to you, do not feel disappointed. Instead, pray, “God, it’s okay if you do not recognize me now. However, I will create a time when you can laugh heartily because of me.” Do not desire to be recognized in a place where God is not pleased.

Pray this way. Therefore, if people recognize you when God does not, feel rather displeased. When doing the same work with ten colleagues of the same level, if you feel that you are the least capable, know what work will be entrusted to you afterward, aside from what you are currently doing, and put in sincerity for that. That is the way to get closer to God.

If you diligently hold early morning prayers for three years for the area you are in charge of, there will surely be a great revival. Evangelize one person each month. When evangelizing, do it one-on-one.

There was an old man who had done much healing through spiritual examination. During that time, a third-generation only child in the area was suffering from tuberculosis, and the parents came to ask this old man to pray for their child. So the old man began to pray, but heaven stopped him. Nevertheless, as the old man persisted, heaven allowed it after receiving the answer that he could pay any price.

Thus, the old man began a hundred-day prayer with sincerity, placing water. Three hours after the hundred-day prayer ended, the water in the cup began to boil, and a voice from heaven was heard. He was told to take the cup of water to the patient, but not to greet or speak to anyone along the way. So the old man ran swiftly with the cup of water and made the patient drink it, and the third-generation only child stood up right there. Shortly after, the old man’s child died in his place.

After his death, Pastor Lee Yong-do appeared to Kim Baek-mun and conducted a mission handover ceremony. The Teacher met Kim Baek-mun in October 1945 and received his blessing. Two months before going to Pyongyang, Seong-jin was born, and the Teacher attended a meeting at Kim Baek-mun's house in Mun-san and was on his way back from that monastery to buy rice when he received God's command to go to North Korea and went straight to Pyongyang.

On August 11, 1946, the Teacher was imprisoned in the Daedong Security Office on charges of fraudulently claiming to be a religious figure by the North Korean Communist Party. While in prison, he was in the same room as Heo Ho-bin, and three days later, he met someone who was in the position of the president of Heo Ho-bin's group in the same cell.

He had already received revelation and offered me a good position, and the next morning he worshipped me. He revealed the internal affairs of Heo Ho-bin's group. Thus, it was as if Chunhyang and Lee Do-ryeong met in prison. They said they had awaited this day, worshipping 7,000 times.

That man was named Hwang Won-sin. The Teacher contacted Heo Ho-bin in prison, risking his life, and urged him to fulfill the responsibility he received through revelation. Later, that fact was discovered, and he was severely punished by the communists.

On June 4, 1946, the Teacher visited the old woman Park, who claimed to be God's wife in the North. At that time, the Teacher began to serve as a servant in Park's house, washing clothes, and even serving towels when going to the bathroom.

During that time, the old woman claimed that the Teacher received a revelation that he was Jehovah but only elevated herself. If at that time the old woman had blessed the Teacher, testified to him, and served and followed him in obedience, the purpose would have been fulfilled.

At that time, the Teacher fought for 40 days. If he yielded in that fight, the restoration providence would have failed. The old woman, who blessed the Teacher but could not serve him, later went mad.

The Teacher stood in the position of having restored Adam's position by receiving the blessings of several men and women. The Teacher has walked the way of the cross of love.

A grandmother who bestows the gift of healing

I will tell a special story about this grandmother. When the teacher went to Pyongyang, who evangelized this grandmother? Was it Ji Seung-do? That’s right? She came to the teacher and shared her life story, the secret stories of heaven, and things she could not tell anyone else in detail. If she told such stories to others, who would listen, thinking she was crazy? So she told everything to the teacher, who knew everything and encouraged her to share it all. Thus, I listened to all those stories. Upon hearing them, it was clear that she had done such remarkable works.

I cannot share all those stories, but I will share just one special story. Because this grandmother performed works of grace, numerous sick people were healed with just her touch, and the news spread not only in Pyongyang but throughout the country. It became such that she could not attend to other matters due to the daily influx of patients. When this grandmother saw a sick person and prayed, saying, "You are healed," they were healed. Such remarkable works occurred, and the news spread throughout the neighboring villages and the entire country. Therefore, patients and even their parents eagerly wished to meet this grandmother.

However, in the neighboring village, a third-generation only son was suffering from tuberculosis, facing a life-and-death situation. Moreover, both his grandmother and mother were widows. The three of them had lived relying on that one son, and how heartbreaking it must have been as he was on the brink of death! Until now, they had used everything they had to save their only son, but if there was any way to save him, they would spare no effort and would devote themselves. So, from some time, the mother and grandmother began to come, asking her to pray for their son or grandson. However, God commanded them not to pray for him. Seeing such things, one might wonder why God would pray for some and not for others, but that is not the case. Such people have a special mission. Those who must be offered as sacrificial offerings for the nation must not be prayed for.

This grandmother did not know. When she prayed to heaven, she was told not to pray for them. Living in the same village, how much did the parents plead with her? Then, as that son was nearly dying, eventually, the mother and grandmother...
It was you who came and wailed. When we are in such a dire situation, it is your responsibility to pray for us, yet you are performing the good of healing the illnesses of countless people, and you wail, asking why you do not pray for our son. Isn't that utterly frustrating on a human level? So, I had no choice but to make a bargaining prayer before God. Since God is a God of love, isn't it natural for me to have a sympathetic heart for such a son? If the Almighty God has a way to extend this son's life, I will do anything, so please let him be healed. I prayed earnestly. As I made this bargaining prayer, God asked me, "If you want that so much, I will grant your wish, but is it okay if I do it my way?" What a joyful statement that was! So, without realizing it, I answered, "Of course." Then God said that for the next 100 days, I should put in my sincerity. The reason I needed to do that was that, according to the principle of restoration through indemnity, that person must fulfill a national sacrificial mission on this earth, and it was to establish that foundation. You may not understand the content of restoration through indemnity well, but in any case, sincerity must be put in.

So, I began the 100-day prayer at Morangbong, where there is a temple called Yongmunsa across from the river Daedonggang, in front of Eulmildae. In the early hours between two and three when no one was around, I went alone to Yongmunsa as a woman and prayed with sincerity for 100 days. No one knew about this. When going to pray, I was instructed not to greet anyone, even if I met my son or my husband. For 100 days, I was to put in that sincerity. I started to put in my sincerity, and even after 99 days, there was no news. Not only that, but on the 100th day, even at two o'clock while praying, there was still no news. How frustrating that must have been! Surely those people would blame God... However, God works around the time when the sun rises, centered on the new morning. For something new to happen, it must be accomplished with bright sunlight. It seems that the grandmother understood this. She thought well that a day begins when the sun rises.

So, she prayed until the dawn passed and the sun rose. As the sun began to rise, a command was given. What was the command? It was to always place clean water when praying. After doing so for 100 days, the command came to look at the water you have drawn. And since the water must be boiling, take that boiling water directly to the patient, and no matter who you meet on the way, do not greet them; go with only one purpose in mind, and when you arrive at that house, even if the mother or grandmother greets you, do not respond but go in and let the young man drink that water, and he will be healed. How joyful that must have been! When thinking that I was bringing a dying life back to God after putting in sincerity for 100 days, how happy I must have been that my wish was coming true! So, I rushed to that house and, not being able to speak, knocked on the door. The mother came out and asked who it was at dawn. No matter how much she asked, I did not respond, but because I knocked so seriously, she opened the door. And there stood the grandmother who had asked for help for her son.

"Oh my, what happened?" she asked. Still, the grandmother ignored that and went into the room where her son was lying sick and gave him the water, and he was healed right then and there. This brought great joy to that household. What kind of joy could there be? So, the three family members shed tears of gratitude, holding onto the grandmother. When morning came and this grandmother was about to return home, would they let her go just like that? Absolutely not; they insisted on holding a feast for her. So, they made rice cakes and even killed a chicken for the feast. After eating, she returned home after two o'clock in the afternoon. When she entered her house, her son had apparently returned early from some business. He had come home first and asked why she was so late today. Normally, she would have returned before five in the morning. She said she was a bit late due to some work and went into the inner room, and her son went upstairs, but as soon as he entered, he complained of a stomachache and lay down, and a few hours later, he died. The only son of that grandmother had died. Only then did the grandmother realize that she had sacrificed her son to save that family's son.

How shocking it must have been for her! Who would have thought that God would do such a thing? When I thought that God would not blame me for doing as I wished, the answer I gave was a hidden meaning. That is, the question was whether I had a loving heart that could exchange my son for that patient if I loved him so much. I answered, "Of course." So, I fulfilled that promise. Thus, I took my eldest son away. 

At this point, how shocking it must have been for this grandmother! Her mind must have been spinning. "God is truly indifferent... You made me testify and reveal God's name before countless people, and there is nothing you have not granted me, yet you take my eldest son away? How could this be? There are so many other people's sons; why must you take mine?" she lamented, but she realized that all of this was her responsibility. 

From that moment on, her mind became strange, and she wandered around aimlessly. It is said that she did this for almost half a year. Until then, she had been respected as a spiritual woman, but now she was wandering around in madness, and rumors spread throughout Pyongyang. There is an intersection called Seomun-bak in Pyongyang, and she wandered there, muttering in despair. Because she was wandering because of him, when he suddenly appeared, she realized at that moment whether it was a dream or reality. So, she had a conversation with her son. What was the conversation? The teacher does not have time to tell all the details. What was said was, "Mother, why are you making it difficult for me?" He then asked, "What is this appearance of yours?" He said he never expected that such a once-great mother would become such a foolish mother. He then scolded her from the top down. I am in a place that is better than the combined place where I can go as a loyal subject recognized by God for the sincerity I devoted while alive and where the person who was healed from illness can go with sincerity on this earth."

Do you understand what that means?
