You must not possess wealth that God does not recognize. The members of the Unification Church all came out like beggars with empty hands. However, they must have at least one set of clothes. But they should think that those clothes are not theirs. If they have more than three sets of clothes, they should take them off and give them to three people. This is the responsibility to find the children of faith.

You know that Jesus washed the feet of His disciples, right? Without establishing such a tradition, you cannot unite them. The teacher has done so. When the teacher heard rumors that the children of enemies were starving, he once gave away everything except for one pair of underwear and a blanket. He lived for a week wearing only the underwear and covering himself with the blanket. Later, he even sold the last remaining blanket for them.

Why did he do such things? It is not because the teacher is lacking. It is because to walk the path of restoration, one must establish the absolute condition of having loved one's enemies. There are not many people in the world who can do such things. However, the teacher sold everything he had for the children of enemies, even selling the last remaining blanket, so he has done enough. He did such things because he must practice the biblical command to love one's enemies.

You must not walk the path of restoration like a rogue. Do you know how the purpose turns? It does not turn as you think. You must recognize once again that to inherit this traditional thought, you must go through a harsh training process. Otherwise, even after a thousand years, it will be useless. You cannot understand traditional thought. Therefore, you must think of everything from that perspective.

The teacher himself does not think of the house he currently lives in or anything else as his own. There is no problem with publicly disposing of anything. Even if the teacher has bank accounts with millions or tens of millions of won, it is not a problem to dispose of them publicly. You must find joy in using it for God rather than for yourself. Absolutely. You must understand that without establishing this absolute standard, you cannot become a heavenly family.

Blessed families should not struggle to survive by doing business or living like others. You must not. Absolutely not. If you acquire money out of selfish desire, you will end up being robbed or losing it later. Otherwise, you will be subjected to robbery. Just wait and see if that is not the case. You must never think of acquiring wealth that God does not recognize. Since the teacher lives this way, you must not live better than the teacher. Isn’t that how it should be? You should not eat better than the teacher or dress better than the teacher. That is the principle. The teacher does not dislike you dressing well or eating well. Pray and find out why the teacher says this.

It is because we live in one household. Because we live in one household, you also eat here. There are many people who would be kicked out in the world. Many people come and go without working and just eat. Yet they pretend not to notice. They all know, but when they see the teacher, they feel ashamed, so the teacher pretends not to notice. Do you have a job? What do you have? That is why you are being fed. After being here for several months, when it comes time to move, some say they have no money and nowhere to go. So, there have been times when the teacher found them a place to live. Why is that? It is because the teacher came to this earth to establish a tradition. It is fine if the teacher has no possessions at all. The teacher must leave behind a tradition. The teacher saves money and does things so that blessed families will not suffer in the future; it is for them.

In the future, money will come in abundance. Therefore, money will not be a problem. You must walk the same path as the teacher. You must think about how to serve God and how to establish a heavenly family as you walk your path.

If you cannot raise sons and daughters who can be loyal to Heaven in place of Jesus, you must understand the teacher's words well. You cannot have children of faith. This is a principle, so unless all 36 families establish children of faith, they cannot enter into tribal formation. When the 7-year course is completed, the 12 tribes will be formed. There are no tribes now, right? There are no tribes. Therefore, the tribes must be formed.

However, only families can join these tribes. Even if it is a family, those that do not establish the conditions of indemnity based on this principled structure at that time will be excluded. I speak frankly. Whether that is the case or not will be known at that time. Do not plead at that time. It will put the teacher in a difficult position.

That time will surely come, so you must at least establish the standard of restoring the family of Adam. If you do not do that, you cannot show your face before God. Therefore, you must prepare quickly before that time comes. That is why I am pushing you. It is because if you do not do it, I must push you to do it.

This activity must be centered on the family. That is why we educate families, hold gatherings centered on families, and engage in activities. If you do so, God will surely work in you just as He did when the teacher started this path. If you have a united heart centered on God's purpose, God will undoubtedly work. You will actually experience this. Then, at that time, you will feel gratitude before God and make a new resolution to take your path. If you do not do this, you may drift away at any time.

That is why you must think of the possessions you have as belonging to the Father. To whom should you dedicate your sons and daughters? You must dedicate them to the Father. If you cannot raise sons and daughters who can be loyal to Heaven in place of Jesus, it cannot be done.

Once you become parents, no matter what you do, your sons and daughters must walk the path of the Unification Church. It cannot be otherwise. And you must also walk the path. You must go first and then teach your children. To educate your children, you must first do it yourself. Only then can you educate your children; trying to educate them without doing it yourself goes against the providence.

Everything the teacher tells you is what the teacher has first practiced to lay the foundation of victory and then teaches you. If you do not believe it, pray about it. Pray to find out if it is a lie or the truth.

That is why you are busy. It is a busy time. Therefore, you must now prepare to evangelize one person each month. Do you understand? If you cannot evangelize one person each month, put in more effort.

Those who have lost children will understand. The heart of a parent who has lost a child, that sorrowful heart cannot be expressed in words. Such parents would do anything if there were a way for that baby to come back to life. With such a desperate heart, put in your effort and evangelize. It will be fine. Knowing that, do not just come next Sunday. Do you understand?

If new leaves do not sprout and new branches do not grow on a tree in spring, it will die. Likewise, if you come into the Unification Church and at first it was good, but new leaves do not sprout and new branches do not grow there, it will die. It will die. If there are no new leaves for more than three years, it will completely die. Therefore, before dying, you must cut the branches and propagate them. If you cut them and stick them in water, they will live and sprout new leaves and new branches, flourishing. What you are going through now is similar to propagating branches.

So do not feel sad when you are sent out from the headquarters church. And when the headquarters church calls you, do not think, "Oh! What good is attending the evening service for three days? Who is preaching today? Ah, I guess I don’t have to go." You must not think that way. Also, do not think, "Oh! Why is that Cheongpadong hill so high? It’s so hot in summer that I feel like I’m dying; why should I go? I should just sleep." If you think that way, you will regret it all. Once you go out, you may want to come back to this Cheongpadong hill, but you will not be able to. Even if you want to come, you cannot come. You cannot come. Do you understand? Those who are being sent out now, understand that? You all must prepare firmly. Do you understand?

Now, let those who want to become members of the Unification Church headquarters and work raise their hands. No, rather, come out this way. Those who want to work, come out this way, and those who want to just observe, come out this way. Men and women, all come out. Let’s count. Stand up quickly. (The recording cuts off here.) 

The significance of the Day of All Things

<Prayer> Father, we know that humanity must eternally praise You as the embodiment of Your being. On the day when Your great work is fulfilled, humanity must achieve all ideals in the realm of Your love with all things and offer eternal honor and praise before You, and we must make it eternally Yours.

Father, we have come to understand the sad fact that the world of joy that could have been ours became the origin of grief for countless ages due to the mistakes of our human ancestors, Adam and Eve. When we think about how this was not due to any external connection but rather through bloodline connections that brought suffering to countless humans, we recognize that we are in a position where we must once again apologize before You for not fulfilling our responsibilities as the masters of all creation. Please allow us to be forgiven.

We understand how much all things have contributed to humanity's restoration until now. We also know that without uniting with all things, we cannot approach You.

Considering the stage of life today, which is connected through families, societies, nations, and the entire world, we recognize that there remains a path of restoration that must be traversed from our current families to the world. Therefore, we have clearly understood through the principle that each of us must fulfill the responsibilities of priests offering substantial offerings that connect all things from our families.

Father, our Unification Church carries the mission of restoration and has the Days of God, Parents, Children, and All Things, which others do not know. Today marks the Day of All Things, which is the seventh year in terms of lunar years and the sixth year in terms of full years. Father, please bless this day.

Today is the first day of the fifth month in the lunar calendar. We reflect on the past when the Day of All Things was established. We think about how this day, which was passed before Heaven in a lonely position that no one welcomed, has become an eternal stepping stone for creating a new historical world and a cornerstone of Heaven.
In the year marking the establishment of the Day of All Things and its third anniversary, we have designated 120 holy sites in 40 countries, representing the nations of the world, to solidify a global foundation either flatly or horizontally. We understand that these connections to holy sites serve as a stepping stone from heaven to restore all things and solidify the foundation of the Day of All Things. We must love all things while also loving the holy sites, and we must be made aware of our responsibility to love all things.

We express our gratitude to our Father, who has paved this path until now. How long have You awaited a day like today to be realized on earth? When we think of this, we must wholeheartedly praise, celebrate, and commemorate this day. Father, we earnestly hope and wish for Your permission.

Father, we know that this universe is the essence of humanity created by You for humankind. When the essence of the human heart, which is You, and the essence of all things, which are the bodies of humanity, are connected centered on humankind, we come to realize that we stand in an immense position as the essence of the microcosm representing the entire cosmos and as the intermediary of heaven.

We are certain that when we speak of heaven, it connects with the incorporeal God, the incorporeal spirit world, and the angelic world, meaning that the entire incorporeal creation is interconnected. Therefore, let us not stop at commemorating this one day, but let this day extend to create brotherly nations that can unite the whole world. Thus, we can establish a peaceful unified world where heaven can dwell within that realm.

Every time we celebrate and commemorate this day, Father, we earnestly wish to be reminded that we must not exceed the standard of our original human ancestors in our ability to love all things. 

Father, please add blessings and grace that You can grant on this day. Moreover, our desire is that the material blessings connect with the people of the nations who love heaven. Since 1969, the new history of restoration has aligned with the direction of the Unification Church centered on this land, the Republic of Korea, and we sincerely hope and wish for a foundation of joy that can symbolize the glory of heaven to be established. Father, please grant this.

We ask that the children scattered across the world be allowed to commemorate this time with their whole hearts and pray before You, and that Your guiding hand and grace may manifest at this time. 

Let joy and glory be with Your children who are present here, and may this day be a day of joy where countless spirits in the spirit world and many martyrs who have borne grievances can also praise Your victory. We earnestly hope and wish for this. Let it be a day of joy that can serve as a condition to resolve their grievances. We offer all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen.

<Words> Today is the 7th Day of All Things. Originally, all things were created for humanity and were to be governed by humanity. However, due to the fall of our human ancestors, Adam and Eve, all things have not been governed by humanity until now, but have been governed by Satan. Because of this, God could not establish a relationship with all things through humanity.

The Day of All Things, which all creation should commemorate and celebrate, has been placed under Satan's dominion due to the fall of our human ancestors, which means that unless we remove Satan's authority that has infringed upon the realm of all things on this earth, all things cannot return to their original position, a fact we understand from a principled perspective.

So, who bears the responsibility to return this Day of All Things to heaven? Since humanity has placed all things under the realm of lamentation, it is humanity that bears the responsibility to liberate all things. This is something God cannot do directly; it is something we must do.

It has been seven years since the Day of All Things was designated on May 1, 1963, and six years in lunar terms. During this time, in 1965, we selected 120 holy sites centered around 40 countries. The reason for selecting holy sites globally is that restoration must now connect the ties of restoration centered on the entire world, rather than just one nation. The ability to select holy sites globally was possible because there was a foundation established in Korea that sought the Day of All Things. If there had been no foundation for establishing the Day of All Things, we would not have been able to select holy sites globally.

Today, the only place that commemorates and observes this Day of All Things is our Unification Church. 

What must be done for this Day of All Things to be established? Because the fall of our human ancestors has caused all things to be placed under Satan's dominion, the true ancestors of humanity must manifest in order to restore all things. Next, we must restore the dominion that God blessed Adam with, centered on the connection of children.

Therefore, we must establish a standard that can govern the entire creation by connecting parents and children horizontally. Thus, in our Unification Church, we have established Parents' Day centered on parents, Children's Day centered on children, and from there, we have established the Day of All Things. This Day of All Things must not remain a day commemorated by just one individual. It must not remain a day commemorated only by blessed families or members of the Unification Church. This Day of All Things must be established as a day celebrated and commemorated by individuals, families, tribes, nations, and the entire creation. Only then can we be assured that we will return to the world we hope for.

Therefore, every time we encounter such a day, we must realize once again that this day must not become a day that we alone commemorate. We must extend this day into a national Day of All Things, which is the immediate task that our Unification Church must resolve.

Moreover, it should not end as a national Day of All Things, but we must advance to the point where the entire nation can establish a global Day of All Things. Thus, centered on God, all of humanity must completely dedicate all things before Him, and unless we establish a standard to restore dominion, we cannot reclaim the dominion over all things that was blessed to Adam and Eve.

Where does the origin of the Day of All Things that you commemorate and celebrate lie? It is connected to the origin of all things centered on the family in which you live. However, that does not mean that all things belong solely to you. That family must be connected to the Unification Church, and centered on the Unification Church, it must connect to unified families, unified tribes, unified nations, and ultimately to a unified world, which must also be connected to this day.

Every item you wear or every essential item you use is part of all things, so you must not regard all essential items in your daily life as remaining within the limits of your own life. You must treat everything as a direct counterpart that reduces the creation of the world and evaluate its value as something global.

Thus, your very life must become a representation of a sacrificial offering, and you must live with the conviction that God can always be present in that sacrificial environment; otherwise, the true familial foundation of all things cannot be established.

Looking at the history of restoration providence, in the Old Testament era, restoration was carried out through offerings. Initially, the providence was to unite with people centered on offerings, and later, it was to unite with God centered on people. This has been the history of restoration providence until now.

From now on, these things must unfold within yourselves. Thus, you must become one with all things in the position of an offering, and then you must become one with God. The history that has been coming down vertically must now be realized horizontally in your families.

Today, all things are under the dominion of Satan, governed in the name of the children of Satan. They are also under the dominion of the nations of the satanic world. This is the reason why God laments and why all things lament. Therefore, we must indemnify and restore this to God's side. For this, the children of God must govern all things centered on God. Not only Adam but also Eve must govern all things that desire to be governed by God. Furthermore, the descendants of our human ancestors, Adam and Eve, must unite to govern all things.

Therefore, blessed families who can govern all things must unite centered on their children and connect them to God. This must not end with families alone; when viewed from the perspective of our Unification Church, it must connect to a unified family, that is, a unified tribe. Moreover, the possessions of Unification Church members must not be limited to those of Unification Church members alone; they must be recognized as the possessions of the nation and the world that the Unification Church desires.

Today, all created beings are in a position of being Satan's because they have been governed through the children of Satan within Satan's dominion. We must return all of this to God's side. From the principled perspective of the path of restoration, all things must first belong to the ancestors of humanity. Of course, it goes without saying that they belong to God, but when viewed from the standard of the blessings that God has given to humanity, they must belong to the ancestors of humanity. In other words, they must belong to the parents of goodness who have not fallen. Next, they must belong to the children of goodness. 

From this perspective, as we celebrate the Day of All Things today, we must always remember that although we have established the Day of God, we have not yet connected all things to a position where God can govern them.

Therefore, the essence of Christian thought today is that when the bridegroom comes, the bride must hold a wedding feast to welcome him. When the wedding feast is held and the bride and bridegroom become one, everything the bride possesses becomes the bridegroom's. In other words, just as a bride entrusts all her possessions to her husband, everything in the created world must not remain as the possessions of individuals. They must go through the stages of restoration until they become God's through True Parents.

You must enter a new nation in the future. However, just as God created all things before creating humanity, all things must first be registered, and then humanity must be registered to connect with God. This historical process corresponds to the 6,000 years of history. In the Old Testament era, it was through all things; in the New Testament era, it was through the Son; and in the era of the Divine Principle, it is through parents that we connect with heaven. All these processes must be traversed.

However, this must not be accomplished only within the limits of our Unification Church today. You must understand that unless this history is expanded beyond the nation to the global realm, we cannot welcome a complete day of restoration.

Restoration cannot be achieved with humanity alone. We have celebrated Parents' Day and Children's Day. However, even with parents and children, complete restoration cannot be achieved. When God blesses humanity, He commands them to be fruitful, multiply, and govern all created beings. Therefore, if there are parents and their offspring, there must be all things that can be governed before them. Thus, we must understand that as we celebrate the Day of All Things, we must first connect all things to heaven centered on families and establish true families, and only then can we connect ourselves to heaven.

Today, you have not yet established a connection with True Parents. Therefore, the blessing that the Unification Church provides is to establish that connection. When a family is established in connection with True Parents, that family must go through the process of connecting to all things. This is why the Day of All Things was designated.

From the day the Day of All Things was established, vertically, there is a family above all things, and above the family is heaven. This must culminate in a single point in the tribe. Horizontally, when the created world was created, first all things were made, then Adam and Eve were created, and then God was present. Therefore, unless this is determined to culminate in a single point both vertically and horizontally, we cannot establish the standard for overall restoration.

For this reason, before we can say that we are the sons and daughters of God, we must first establish the condition that everything we possess belongs to God. You must understand that this must be established before the second seven-year course passes.

The first seven-year course is the period for establishing the standard to go as parents, and the second seven-year course is the period for establishing the standard to go as children. Therefore, when the second seven-year course ends, a new tribal formation must emerge. At that time, everything belonging to the blessed family will not be the possession of that family alone. It will be the possession of the world, the nation, the Unification Church, and all the family members, and then it will become mine. In other words, it will be the possession of the world on a large scale and mine on a small scale. You must understand that this process must be traversed.

Therefore, from now on, an era of inheritance centered on all things must come. Following that, an era of registration centered on families must come. Only when we can register to the standards of tribe, nation, and country can God dwell in that nation. When families that have gone through such connections are linked to a society, and that society is linked to a nation, only then can that nation become one that God can govern.

You must learn to regard all material things as public. What you must understand as Unification Church members is that everything you have owned until now, or your possessions, are in the process of being managed temporarily. In other words, you are managers. Each of you must manage well and offer these all things before God, which must return to God's embrace through the embrace of True Parents. In other words, you must clearly understand that without passing through the process of being God's and True Parents' possessions, they cannot become yours.

Based on the customs you have lived by on this earth until now, you may claim something as belonging to you, but you must not remain there. All of this must pass through the names of parents and God. Only then can the standard of restored all things be completed.

Therefore, until you reach such a day, you are not the owner but the manager. Thus, you must fulfill your responsibilities as a manager until the time you return it to the owner.

From this perspective, you must clearly distinguish between public and private. However, is the human heart like that? We often see this in our Unification Church; when it comes to public things, people generally neglect them. Moreover, in the Unification Church...
If it is something public that belongs to the headquarters, it is the property of many Unification Church members within this headquarters jurisdiction. Compared to personal belongings, it holds a broader scope of content and value. When we first offer this to God, that is, when we offer public property first, all private belongings will be completely offered as well.

From this perspective, you must orderly distinguish between the public property of the Unification Church and your private belongings. Through such a process, you should clarify the standards of private and public, and learn to live centered on solid principles. However, generally, it seems to be the opposite. Private belongings are cherished, while public property is neglected. This absolutely cannot be the case. You must learn to value public property.

In order to overcome the peak of restoration of all things through our private belongings, we must first transform them into public property, whether for the church, the nation, or even the world. Therefore, you must understand that public property should be prioritized.

From this standpoint, what kind of lifestyle should we Unification Church members have? We must abandon the ownership mindset that considers everything as personal belongings. Therefore, at some point, we will discuss issues centered around this problem. There are various surnames like Kim and Park, but those surnames must eventually be unified. We must go through a new lineage centered on the True Parents.

**The Standard for Complete Restoration of All Things**

When viewed from this perspective, people are more important than things, and God is more important than people. Today's humans say, "I am the best," centered on themselves, but there is no hope for world restoration centered on oneself. People are more important than things, and heaven is more important than people. We must learn to see all things centered on heaven.

Complete restoration cannot be achieved by restoring just oneself. Only after becoming one with heaven and then completely uniting with external things can we say, "This is heaven's." Only then can we stand in a position to claim ownership. You must understand that this process remains in the path you must take.

From this perspective, a time will come when even the wealthiest chaebols in the Republic of Korea will not be able to exist in a position where they can solely own and enjoy their wealth. Before it becomes theirs, it must first belong to God, and furthermore, to the True Parents. Without this, it cannot become theirs. Today's Unification Church members must thoroughly embrace this mindset. However, until now, this mindset has not been thoroughly established among us. Now, every time we face the Day of All Things, we must think anew about all things. We must also universalize this concept. We must realize that without feeling the necessity of going through this process, there is no significance in celebrating the Day of All Things.

Therefore, we must elevate our possessions to that level and go through public connections. Thus, we must establish material connections through ourselves. To do this, we must create a foundation that can quickly restore the Republic of Korea by going through higher standards of material connections than small ones.

Whether as individuals or in expanding private property, in other words, whether in earning money or having an attachment to material things, we must go through such standards. This must be generalized.

However, people living in today's fallen world all claim ownership based on their habits and concepts. You must understand that this is not acceptable. Therefore, you must go through this process centered on your family today, and also centered on the Unification Church.

The church's property is more important than individual property, the nation's property is more important than the church's, and the world's property is even more important than the nation's. All future possessions must ultimately become the world's possessions. At the same time, they must become God's possessions on a global scale, True Parents' possessions on a global scale, and True Children's possessions on a global scale. We have the responsibility to restore all things to such possessions. You must feel this deeply every time you celebrate the Day of All Things.

You must understand that if all things I possess remain only in my embrace, they cannot escape the realm of lamentation. They must not be under my name. They must pass through God's name.

The same goes for you. Do not think of yourselves as just Kim or Park. Until now, it has been unavoidable, but in the future, you must stand in a position that acknowledges you have come through your parents' names. This does not mean that everyone should become a Moon family following the name of the Unification Church's founder. Rather, you must live with the mindset that you possess such content and have a second name. You must all go through this process.

All things must pass through the name of the parents and the name of God. Humans must also be registered in heaven and must go through the emotional connections of the parents and God's emotional connections; otherwise, we cannot claim to have established the standard of a complete restoration family. You must understand that a society where family matters can be handled freely in the church and church matters can be handled freely in the nation is what we call a heavenly society.

I hope you feel once again that you are the ones who must resolve such matters within your living sphere at some point. Please recognize that today is indeed the Day of All Things.

**Prayer**: Father, we have come to understand that our human ancestors were meant to become one through the love connection with You and the love of their spouses. We have realized that all things should have been united in the love centered on the Father and the ancestors of humanity. However, due to the fall of humanity, all things have entered the realm of lamentation, and we know that You are also lamenting.

Looking back at the course of the providence of restoration, we see that in order to restore humanity, all things were presented before them. They were to become one with all things and connect with You at the center to achieve unity.

However, while we have connected such relationships centered on individuals, today, we cannot do so with individuals alone in our Unification Church. Because the ancestors of humanity fell before forming a couple, we must complete a standard that can connect couples with You. All things centered on that couple must inevitably pass through Your name and the name of the True Parents, and we must clearly understand that a new task remains.

We must recognize that without going through this, we could not have been created today. Just as we were formed through good things and things belonging to You, all things can only achieve unity with You and the True Parents when they surpass a certain boundary. We earnestly hope that You will allow us to understand that the source of global standards is established centered on families in today's flat world.

We have not devoted ourselves to the things that can achieve this. As individuals who eat, use, and manage, we have not lived a life of devotion to offer those things completely before You. We know that there must be a day when we can sequentially connect these from family relationships to national relationships to world relationships and offer them before You. At that time, through families, tribes, nations, and the world, all of humanity must celebrate a day when they offer all their ownership and their entire families before You. In other words, we must understand that the day of registration into heavenly families must be established.

When that day comes, countless people will compete to praise that joyful day, and a realistic stage will appear on earth where they can compete to offer that day to You as a heavenly day, thus breaking all the conditions of lamentation that You have endured for 6,000 years, leaving only the historical hope that You can rejoice. Please allow them to understand this clearly.

Father, to welcome that day, please allow us to offer everything we have before You, and let us dedicate our bodies and families entirely before You. Thus, let us understand that we must inherit the eternal heritage as heirs through the love of the heavenly parents, namely the True Parents, and let us recognize the tremendous mission that lies upon us.

We know that such things must happen personally, as well as on the family, tribe, nation, and world levels. We earnestly hope that You will allow us to be children who understand that in order for this to happen globally, we must conduct ceremonies of separation and connect everything to heaven.

Father, there are blessed families present here. We must realize when we have passed such conditions before You and when we have established the conditions of the original substance centered on Your love. We understand that we have not yet established such conditions, and we earnestly hope that You will help us realize that we are in the process of establishing such foundations nationally and globally.

Today, we hope to make a new resolution to achieve such purposes and to create such dramatic moments and times, allowing us to celebrate this day.

Children across the nation are celebrating this day. We earnestly hope that by aligning with Your power, ability, and authority, the day of liberation for all things may come soon. Along with this, may the day come quickly when Your beloved children can return to You, centered on any nation, and create a second realm of liberation. We earnestly ask for this, and we pray all these words in the name of the True Parents. Amen.
